A 77-Year-Old Man Fell and Died in Front of His Ancestral Grave While Sweeping the Tomb

Wang Shengbao, a 77-year-old boatman from the Yunyunbang in Wusong, had an eldest son, Baogen, and his wife, Zhao; and a second son, Baobao, and his wife, Xie. Wang Shengbao moved his family's houseboat to Wangjia Wharf in southern Shanghai to make it easier for his two sons to return home, as they were both sailors on the Longda and Hongda ships of the Shanghai Datong Shipping Company. However, Wang's ancestral grave was located in front of the Huoshaomiao Temple near the Hujiazhuang in western Song. The day before yesterday was Qingming, and Wang Shengbao, as his sons, daughters-in-law, and others were all busy and did not have time to sweep the tombs, took his 11-year-old grandson, named Maogou, alone to Wusong, hired a shanban boat to go to Hujiazhuang to sweep the tomb. After the offerings were completed, as the old man was about to step off the sampan, he accidentally fell on the field embankment. Unexpectedly, this fall led to his death. When the sampan rower caught a glimpse, he rushed forward to check and saw the old man lying stiff and unresponsive. Upon closer inspection, he had stopped breathing and died. Therefore, he immediately returned to Song and rushed to Shanghai to report to his sons Baogen and Baobao and their entire families. Yesterday, they arrived in Song to prepare a coffin and collect the body. It is said that the old man was usually strong and healthy, with no illnesses, but he was stubborn, so the boatmen all called him a "foreigner."

Going Abroad Without a Passport

Ship Sailors Catch "Yellowfish"

Seven People Were Found on a Ship to Japan

Leaving the country to go abroad requires government approval and the issuance of a passport before purchasing a ticket and boarding a ship. This is the proper procedure. However, recently, there have been some unscrupulous elements who have taken advantage of the difficulty in obtaining a passport and the high cost of ship tickets to secretly set up so-called "catch (pronounced kua in the Ningbo dialect) yellowfish" organizations. They collude with sailors or waiters on various ships to solicit passengers who do not qualify for a passport or cannot afford a ticket. They charge a certain package fee (cheaper than the ship ticket) and hide these people in the coal bunkers of the ship. They do not come out during the journey, and food is secretly provided. Upon arrival in a foreign country, they pretend to be sailors on the ship and secretly go ashore. Generally, each ship takes about ten people on each voyage, and the government and the shipping company are unaware. It is said that this secret organization is located in the Hongkou area and makes a good profit. Recently, seven people from Wenzhou, including Ye Qicheng (29 years old), Zhang Jiabao (23 years old), Wang Zhenlin (25 years old), Wang Fushan (45 years old), Zhao Wensheng (30 years old), Xu Yaren (34 years old), and Jin Shanxian (40 years old), were farming in their hometowns. They were lured by others, saying that they could go to Japan to work, where the wages were high and it would not be difficult to get rich. Ye and others were ignorant and believed it. However, they were afraid that they would not qualify when applying for a passport, so they entrusted this secret organization to find a way. They were hidden in the coal bunkers of the Blue Funnel Line ship that was about to leave for Japan in order to leave the country with the ship. Unexpectedly, their plan was discovered, and someone secretly reported it to the Customs Water Police Station. Detectives Qu Hequei and Xu Leniang boarded the ship and found them. The hiding place was in the interlayer of the coal bunker, and those hidden were very distressed. However, without inside information, it would be difficult to detect. The seven people were taken to the police station. After questioning, it was found that they were foolishly deceived, which was very pitiful. They were sent to the District Court for disposition.

In the Pursuit of Thieves, a Stray Bullet Hit a Passerby Who Died

A Thief with More Than Ten Gunshots Wounds Did Not Die

A Passerby Was Fatally Wounded by a Stray Bullet

At 7:45 PM last night, a major case occurred at the intersection of Avenue Dubail and Rue Montauban in the French Concession, where many passersby were killed and injured by stray bullets during the pursuit of thieves. The details are as follows:

A Young Man with a Gun

At 7:45 PM last night, at the intersection of Rue Xu Jia Hui and the border of the Chinese Concession in the French Concession, the sound of police whistles was suddenly heard. At the same time, a young man, about 20 years old, wearing a black cotton robe and holding a handgun, was running north on Rue Xu Jia Hui and darted into Rue Montauban. Seeing that someone was chasing him, the young man fired a shot into the air as a warning, fleeing and firing at the same time, until he reached the entrance of the Meiya Silk Weaving Factory.

Three Policemen Chased Together

At the entrance of the factory, a Chinese policeman from the No. 366 reserve team stationed by the police station heard the alarm and rushed out with a gun. At the same time, Xie Huiqing from No. 2 Third Tao and a Western policeman from No. 166 happened to be passing by. They all joined together to chase the thief. The three policemen concentrated their gunfire on the thief's lower body, and the shots were as dense as a string of pearls. Passersby scattered and fled. The thief also returned fire and resisted arrest.

Falling to the Ground to Be Captured

The thief fled and fired, but he had been hit by more than ten bullets in his lower body, arms, and legs. His strength gradually weakened, but he still staggered into Fugui Lane. As soon as he entered the alley entrance, he fell to the ground and was captured. First, the Western policeman from No. 2 bravely stepped forward and snatched the thief's gun. At the same time, the police station had heard the news and dispatched a large number of Chinese and Western detectives who arrived one after another and took the thief to the police station.

No Possessions

After arriving at the police station, the thief was searched thoroughly. Apart from the handgun and clothes, he had no possessions. He confessed his name as Han Hongqing, 27 years old, from Gaoqiao, Pudong. His other statements were vague. Upon closer inspection, although the thief had been hit by more than ten bullets, none were vital. He was sent to the hospital for treatment first. However, the police station examined the route he had taken and believed that he had fled from the Chinese Concession into the French Concession. They sent detectives to the Liyuan Road Police Station of the Second District to inquire, but the police station absolutely denied that a thief-catching incident had occurred within its jurisdiction.

One Passerby Was Killed

When the two sides were firing at each other, Ma Genquan, a 25-year-old Pudong native living at No. 25 Tanjiazhai on Luban Road in the Chinese Concession, happened to be passing by. A stray bullet hit him in the chest, and he fell to the ground and died immediately. Zheng Guisheng (52 years old), the owner of the nearby Xietai Coal Store, who was walking in front of the door with his young son in his arms, was also hit in the arm by a stray bullet. A Vietnamese policeman from the No. 84 French Police Station was also grazed in the arm by a stray bullet while pursuing the thief. The injured were sent to the hospital for treatment, while the body of the deceased Ma Genquan was sent to the coroner's office by the police station after notifying the Tongren Fuyuan branch to wait for a report to the Second Special Court for examination.

Selling Smuggled Cigarettes

Fined 5,000 Yuan and Cigarettes Confiscated

The Original Judgment Was Upheld After the Appeal

Zhou Baosheng and Zhu Qiming, detectives from the Cigarette Inspection Office of the French Concession of the National Government's Ministry of Finance's Cigarette Consolidated Tax, discovered on February 28th of last year that the Lianhe Cigarette Company in the Xingonghexing Tobacco and Paper Store at 549 Avenue Edward VII was selling smuggled cigarettes. They reported to Western Detective Wu Yaoou, who reported to the Second Special District District Court to issue a search warrant and went to the company to search and seize 1,302 smuggled cigars and five purchase ledgers, which were taken back to the police station. Later, the ledgers were sent to the Suzhou-Zhejiang-Anhui Cigarette Consolidated Tax Inspection Office. After investigation by staff member Ling Yin Song, the company sold a total of 3,897.5 boxes of smuggled cigars from February 29, 1932, to January 24, 1933, evading a tax of 4,226.81 yuan. The company's manager, Zhang Chengsheng (57 years old, Ningbo native), was summoned to the Second Special District Court. The police lawyer prosecuted him according to Articles 3 and 4 and Penalties 1 and 2 of Article 20 of the Ministry of Finance's Regulations on the Collection of Cigarette Consolidated Tax. After trial, it was ruled that Zhang Chengsheng was selling smuggled cigarettes, and a penalty was imposed, and the smuggled cigarettes were confiscated. Zhang Chengsheng was dissatisfied with the penalty and filed an appeal, which was approved, and the original penalty was revoked, and the case was retried. Yesterday, Judge Wu Fanglian held a trial in Criminal Court Eight. Police Lawyer Lih Jiahuah appeared in court. The defendant Zhang Chengsheng arrived in court with his defense lawyer. After a detailed trial in court, it was ruled that Zhang Chengsheng should still be punished according to the original penalty, paying a fine of 5,000 yuan, and the smuggled cigarettes would be confiscated.

MGM Filming "The Good Earth"

Has Been Approved by the Central Government

MGM of the United States came to Shanghai a month ago, wanting to adapt Pearl S. Buck's novel [The Good Earth] into a film. They submitted the script to the Central Government for review. The Central Propaganda Department and the Film and Drama Review Committee reviewed it and found that the script depicted bandits and other situations in China, which was inaccurate, and it was not approved. Later, the company requested the Central Government to revise the script so that it was completely different from Buck's original work and requested the Central Government to send people to supervise the filming at all times. After several weeks of discussion, the script was revised. The content expressed the spirit of China's inherent culture as much as possible, as well as the development of national rejuvenation, which was in line with the spirit of the times. The Central Government has now appointed Du Tingzhi and Huang Ying to come to Shanghai to guide everything and has notified the local authorities to provide protection and convenience. It is said that filming has begun today.

Municipal Council Discusses the Question of Retaining or Abolishing the Music Corps

To be Presented to the Annual Taxpayers' Meeting

At the Municipal Council meeting on the 4th of this month, during the discussion of this year's budget, a certain director raised the question of retaining or abolishing the music corps. A certain director stated that it is difficult to increase municipal taxes this year, and the budget balance depends solely on drawing funds (two million yuan) from the general reserve fund. After this amount is withdrawn, only 550,000 yuan will remain in the general reserve fund. It is concerning how next year's budget will be balanced. Before making a request to taxpayers to increase taxes, the council should exercise the greatest possible economy. Although the preparation of this year's budget has already been done with tight restrictions, the music corps still exists, which is inconsistent with this. He proposed that at this year's Taxpayers' Annual Meeting, the council should propose abolishing the corps on the grounds of financial difficulty, as the education plan for this year has already been changed due to a shortage of funds. It is inappropriate to spend 300,000 yuan annually to maintain the music corps. After discussion, the majority of the directors agreed to submit a formal motion at the Taxpayers' Annual Meeting and to include a section on abolishing the music corps in the Chairman's speech so that taxpayers can express their opinions.

Special Item

New Life Movement Week Work Plan

I. General Principles (1) Based on the resolution of the general meeting, April 9th is designated as School Day, the 10th as Labor Day, the 11th as Business Day, the 12th as Agriculture Day, the 13th as Government Day, the 14th as Family Day, and the 15th as General Public Day. (2) For the above-mentioned movement days, the General Association will send letters to relevant agencies and organizations to assist in handling them. (3) The General Association will send letters to the Second Regiment of the Military Police and the Public Security Bureau, and the Boy Scouts Council, to dispatch personnel to form a discipline team, which will persuade pedestrians to pay attention to the New Life in the important places of the streets. (4) Propaganda materials will be distributed by the General Association, but various agencies and organizations should also make their own imitations to seek universality. (5) The General Association will hold film propaganda and broadcast lectures to promote propaganda. (6) When necessary, various agencies and organizations may also add items outside of the various items stipulated in this plan. First Day (April 9th) School Day (1) When holding the memorial week of the Prime Minister, each school will report on the significance of the New Life Movement and read out the New Life Covenant. (2) A general cleaning will be held in the school. (3) Check whether the students' bodies, clothes, desks and chairs, and homework supplies are clean. (4) Select students to organize a propaganda team to promote the New Life Movement in the vicinity. (5) Arrange the New Life environment in the school. (6) Primary schools should use "Teaching of Implementing the New Life" as a unit. (7) The principal or staff of the autonomous association will solicit members for the Promotion Association and prepare to organize a branch. (8) Supervise the commuting students to promote the New Life Covenant to their families. (9) The General Association and the Education Bureau will send personnel to inspect the progress of each school. Second Day (April 10th) Labor Day (1) The General Labor Union will convene worker representatives to give speeches on the significance of the New Life Movement and read out the New Life Covenant. (2) The factory will hold a general cleaning to seek cleanliness. (3) Paste New Life slogans inside and outside the factory and arrange the New Life environment. (4) The staff of the District Labor Union or branch office will guide the lives of the members of the Labor Union and strive for their rules and cleanliness. (5) The factory owner or the person in charge of the labor union will solicit members of the Promotion Association and prepare to organize a branch. Third Day (April 11th) Business Day (1) The Municipal Chamber of Commerce will convene businessmen to hold a New Life Movement speech meeting and read out the New Life Covenant. (2) Each store will hold a general cleaning. (3) Store owners check the clothes of the shop assistants and pay attention to their cleanliness and simplicity. (4) New Life Movement slogans are posted everywhere in the storefronts and hotel entrances. (5) Store owners solicit shop assistants to join the New Life Movement Promotion Association. Fourth Day (April 12th) Agriculture Day (1) The Municipal Farmers' Association will convene farmers to hold a New Life Movement lecture meeting and read out the New Life Covenant. (2) New Life Movement slogans are posted all over the agricultural areas. (3) Farmers' clothes and bodies should pay attention to their cleanliness, which will be guided by people sent by the district farmers' association. (4) A general cleaning will be held in the rural areas. (5) The District Farmers' Association will lead the solicitation of farmers to join the New Life Movement Promotion Association. Fifth Day (April 13th) Political circles (1) Party, government and military organs will hold separate general cleanings, and the following matters should be noted. (A) The internal and external rooms, windows and walls of each organ should be cleaned. (B) The documents and books in the office of each organ should be checked and cleaned. (C) Check that the soldiers' clothes and dormitories should pay attention to their cleanliness. (2) The heads of each organ will lead the solicitation of staff to join the New Life Movement Promotion Association. Sixth Day (April 14th) Family Day (1) Each household will hold a general cleaning, paying attention to the following matters. (A) Clean the rooms, windows and walls. (B) Wash the bedding. (C) Children's clothes and bodies should pay attention to cleanliness. (D) The floors inside and outside the house and the roads in front of and behind the door should be cleaned. (2) The city's boy scout organization will organize propaganda teams to promote door-to-door. (3) The city's girls' schools should organize propaganda teams separately on this day and promote door-to-door. The school authorities shall be responsible for the organization and shall report the progress of the work to the Municipal Education Bureau for assessment. Seventh Day (April 15th) General Public Day (1) A general public meeting will be held to give speeches on the New Life Movement and read out the New Life Covenant. (2) A city-wide street cleaning will be held, with the Sanitation Bureau responsible for the Chinese area and the Public Works Department responsible for the concession area. (3) In the city's villages, neighborhoods, and streets, the landlord shall order the gatekeeper to clean up and pay attention to the fact that garbage should not be dumped on the ground. (4) New Life Movement slogans are posted everywhere inside and outside the city's trams, buses, rickshaws, and playgrounds. New Life Movement slogans are posted and played inside and outside cinemas. Please ask the Railway Bureau to post the same slogans in the trains. (5) Military police, police and boy scouts organize discipline teams to check citizens' clothes and advise them to pay attention to cleanliness. (6) The party and national flags are hung all over the city. (7) A lantern parade will be held in the evening, and the method will be formulated separately.

Letter

Sir, I am writing to inform you that Chen Jialu, the owner of Ruiyou Tian Fuzhou Food Store, No. 1376, Edward Road, Shanghai, is an honest Fuzhou merchant. The store has been open for more than ten years. The Hongwan case in Junle Village was solved by Xiao Zhang and others who lived together and has nothing to do with the store. However, in your newspaper's report on April 5th, you mistakenly believed that the store was involved and even exaggerated the facts. This has a significant impact on business credit and personal reputation. As a lawyer, in order to protect the legal rights of merchants and uphold the reputation of your newspaper, I urgently request a correction and provide evidence below. (1) Ruiyou Tian Store has been open for more than ten years, while the room at the front of the house has only been rented for more than a month. (2) After investigation by the police, it was found that it has nothing to do with Ruiyou Tian Store. (See the news of the day's trial.) (3) Chen Jialu, the owner of the store, is from Fuzhou, while most of those who live and visit the front room are from Shantou, Guangdong, not the Fujian gang, nor are there any Fuzhou people. (4) The years of leasing and usual behavior can be investigated by the second landlord and the neighbors on the left and right. (5) The goods wholesaled by the store are sold by major companies and stores and have nothing to do with the operation of Hongwan. Based on the above points, a detailed investigation can be made, and it is not difficult to find out the truth. Please, your newspaper, uphold justice and extend the snow, and immediately correct and proclaim it in the newspaper to avoid slander and maintain commerce, which is a great convenience. Sincerely, to the editor of Shen Bao, Lawyer Shen Xiaoxiang, April 6th.

To the honorable Editor of Shen Bao, I read in your newspaper this morning that the Asia Editorial Office threatened Ma Zhanshan, which involved my name. Some of the facts are slightly inconsistent. Now, I will add a supplementary description in order, and please publish it in the newspaper for correction. In February this spring, I received a letter from my friend General Ma Zhanshan, saying that someone named Ma, No. 4 Sande Lane, Xiafei Road, Shanghai, sent a letter of intimidation, the wording of which was similar to extortion, and asked me to investigate. (The threatening letter has now been sent to the plaintiff's lawyer.) I immediately went to the address in the letter to investigate. The place was an empty house with no one living there, so I replied to General Ma, saying that this kind of thing happens often and that he should not mind. A few days later, I received another letter from General Ma, saying that the intimidator had sent another letter of intimidation and sent a "Sample of Ma Zhanshan's Little Biography," which was full of slander and said that it would be published in the Asia Editorial Office, and asked me to investigate again. Because I was busy with affairs and unfamiliar with Shanghai addresses, I immediately sent the original letter and the "Sample of Ma Zhanshan's Little Biography" to Mr. Du Yuesheng and asked him to send someone to investigate. Mr. Du then entrusted Mr. Tang Shichang to investigate. Later, I heard Mr. Yuesheng tell me that the person had been found. According to himself, he pretended to be a former part of the General, and because he had no livelihood, he had to do this. At that time, Mr. and Mr. Yuesheng both thought that if it was indeed a former part of General Ma, and he had been resisting Japan for many years, although the matter was unwarranted, it was still pitiful. We could afford to bear the cost of some living expenses. I wrote to General Ma, and Mr. Yuesheng entrusted Mr. Tang to persuade them tactfully. The three negotiations at the Great East Hotel mentioned in your newspaper may refer to this. Several days later, they asked for 100,000 yuan for living expenses. Later, I received a letter from General Ma, saying that his subordinates did not have such a rogue. Someone came to Shanghai to file a lawsuit. At this point, Mr. and Mr. Yuesheng had no choice but to give up and ignore it. Then, I read in the newspaper a few days ago that the French Public Works Bureau copied a letter from me to Mr. Du Yuesheng and a letter from General Ma to me at Wang Haiqiu's place. I was very shocked because I had no dealings with Wang Haiqiu, and I thought it must be fabricated. I wanted to publish a statement in the newspaper. The French Public Works Bureau sent someone to bring the letter to confront me. After reading it, I realized that the wording was indeed the same as the original letter, or it was copied by Wang Haiqiu at Mr. Tang's place. Regarding the matter, I have detailed everything to the Second Court of the Jiangsu Special Zone yesterday. As for whether Wang Haiqiu and others are subordinates of General Ma, whether General Ma has embezzled the donations he has received, General Ma and Wang Haiqiu, etc., each have their own methods to defend themselves, and there is no need for me to say more. However, the original letters of intimidation sent to me by General Ma are indeed different from those published in your newspaper. This point should also be solemnly declared. (All the letters of intimidation have been sent to the plaintiff's lawyer for corroboration.) In this era of rampant human desires and confusion between right and wrong, I am naturally unwilling to reverse black and white and disrupt the world's vision. I have always admired your newspaper's strict arguments and advocacy of fairness. In order to record each section of the case related to me one by one, I respectfully ask you to publish it quickly. To be the most grateful for public friendship. This congratulates you on your writing. From Du Chongxuan, April 7th.

Reading Q&A

The Marriage Problem Expressed in Little Ten Years

Reading Guidance

Letter

A letter was received proposing Mr. Ye Yongzhen's book, The Marriage Problem Expressed in Little Ten Years. Although the editor read this book many years ago, the impression left is already very thin: and there is no book at hand to refer to, so I don't want to make any criticisms casually for the time being (if the reader needs it, it can be criticized), now I will only explain the two opinions you collected [and your own] [explanation].

We think that the two opposite opinions you put forward both have considerable reasons on the surface, but in reality they are equally wrong. Why? Because if any problem is not solved from its social roots, but only circles around the problem itself, a correct conclusion can never be reached. This means that they have not grasped the core of the marriage problem or the love problem.

The marriage problem is a social problem, and its change is determined by the change of society. In a male-centered society, women are slaves and spoils of war, and marriage becomes a transaction; in a capitalist society, as you said, everything is commodified, and women are no exception. Although there is so-called free love in form, this love is built on money, as well as the vanity, deception, and promiscuity caused by money. Saying this does not ignore the importance of the marriage problem to life, but rather points out the importance of understanding it from a social point of view. To abolish the marriage of buying and selling, it is not successful to eliminate the remaining feudal forces; to enjoy true free love, it is also not successful to change the private property system. This point is not the question you want to ask, but it is the starting point for solving general problems. (To be continued)

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

The Origin of Children's Day

— Da Qi

The origin of Children's Day is that the Shanghai Children's Care Association petitioned the National Government in the 20th year of the Republic of China to set the festival on April 4th. After the government approved it, this year is the third year, just like a child who is three years old. The term Children's Day originated in foreign countries. For example, Children's Day in the United States is on May 1st, and the second week of December is called the Happy Day for Poor Children. The United Kingdom sets July 14th as Children's Day, and Children's Day in Japan is divided into two days for boys and girls. March 3rd is set as Girls' Day, and May 5th is set as Boys' Day. No matter which country's children, on this day, lectures are held all over the country to discuss children's issues, how to improve them, and how to seek happiness? There are also amusement fairs to provide entertainment for children on this day. The fathers and mothers of children all over the country give their children new clothes to wear, just like the usual festival situation in our country. What is particularly special is that the White House in the United States is open on Children's Day, and children can freely go in and play. When the President sees them, he also shakes hands with many children, and the President sends a bag of candy and a book to everyone who goes to the White House to play!

We Chinese also recognize that children are the masters of the future, so we learn from foreign countries and set April 4th as Children's Day, one is to awaken the people of the whole country to pay attention to children, and the other is to promote the children of the whole country to reflect on themselves: how much they expect of children by valuing them so much!

Boy Scouts

— Yan Chonglou

I want to be a Boy Scout:

I don't want to wear that pointed felt hat, that neat short uniform, tie that green tie, or hang that bright badge.

I don't want to live in that open-air camp, sing those joyful songs, eat that self-cooked wild game, or play those group games.

I love group life: I love the little friends all over the world even more. They are all my brothers and sisters: we want the same work! The same rest! The same enjoyment!

We do not avoid dangers or fear difficulties. We often go to the fields to catch pests, and often go to the mountains and forests to hunt wild animals. When we encounter rivers blocking our way, we build bridges to pass; when we encounter pits and ditches hindering us, we work together to fill and level them. In the dark night, we light torches to make the darkness as bright as the daytime.

We want to accomplish great undertakings, we want to find the true meaning of life, we hold hands and advance bravely, and we will eventually achieve final victory.

We want to be a team of brave Boy Scouts!

Several Diligent and Hard-Studying People in Ancient Times

— Wu Jinhua

Children: Are you diligent in your schoolwork? Now, I will introduce you to several [diligent and hard-studying people in ancient times]. First, [Kuang Heng] was extremely studious, but because his family was poor, he often chiseled through the wall of his neighbor's house to draw light and read. Second, [Zhu Maichen] was also extraordinarily studious. Before he became successful, he carried firewood to the market, forgetting to sell it because he was reading. Third, [Sun Kang]'s family was too poor to afford oil lamps, so he often borrowed the reflected light of snow to read. Fourth, [Sun Jing], fearing that he would fall asleep and abandon his studies, tied his hair to a beam above his head while reading. Fifth, [Cheng Gong] herded pigs as a child. He happened to pass by a school and, hearing the sound of reading, went inside to ask the teacher to teach him. He was allowed to attend, and he studied extremely hard, later becoming a great Confucian scholar. Su Qin loved to read. Whenever he felt sleepy, he would stab his thigh with an awl. Eventually, his studies were completed, and he became the prime minister of six states.

Children: The above are several diligent scholars. Do you want to become great people like them? Then, you should study hard.

Big sister hits little brother!

Resistance

— Bo Zhen

The hateful winter has finally gone, and the welcome spring has arrived. At this time, everything on the earth shows the signs of revival. Especially in the fields in the countryside, the lush green vegetables bloom with golden flowers, swaying with the wind. The red sun is gradually sinking towards the west.

At this time, a fire-yellow snake is coiled in the messy weeds, searching for food.

Here, "ge ge ge" is calling loudly, and there, "ge ge ge" is answering, turning a quiet countryside into a bustling place.

The big snake wanted to eat the frogs, so it sneaked over and swallowed a small frog whole. The rest of the frogs fled for their lives.

Seeing their companion being snatched away by the robber-like snake, the frogs held a temporary meeting. A larger and smarter frog proposed: "Our companion has been snatched away by the robber. If we continue like this, and don't rise up to resist, I'm afraid we will become extinct, and we will have nowhere to live." Then, one frog said: "We are weak and small. How can we resist that ferocious robber!" Another frog thought for a while, stood up and said: "It doesn't matter, as long as we can unite, be consistent with the outside world, fight the robber desperately, and resist to the end, we will definitely achieve victory." Everyone agreed, and they were determined to unite. Sure enough, they subdued the robber-like snake as if it had been ironed with an iron.

The Bucket with a Bottom and the Bucket Without a Bottom

— White Goose

Once upon a time, there was a very wealthy man who had a lot of family property. People said that he came from a very poor background. Therefore, a poor man also wanted to become wealthy like him. One day, when there was an opportunity, he asked the wealthy man to teach him the method of getting rich.

The wealthy man was very polite, but he did not teach him immediately. He only said: "I have no method. If you trust me, then take these two buckets to fetch water. Today, use the one with the bottom to fetch water and the one without the bottom to hold it." As he spoke, he took out two wooden buckets of the same size, one with a bottom and one without a bottom.

The poor man listened to him. He fetched water until evening, but there was no water in the bucket at all, because the water fetched with the bucket with the bottom immediately flowed out when it was put into the bucket without the bottom. He told the wealthy man the result. The wealthy man said: "Very good, tomorrow you do the opposite. Let the bucket with the bottom hold and the one without the bottom fetch." The poor man did as he was told again. As a result, the bucket with the bottom was full, because even though there were only two or three drops of water fetched each time, over time, there was more. Then, the wealthy man smiled and said: "This is my method of getting rich! My wealth is not because I can earn a lot of money, but because I can save the money I earn. Conversely, if I can earn a lot but spend it all, isn't it the same as not earning it?"

The Benefits of Savings

Hide your money well!

I hide it in the savings jar

Mom, don't use it

Use your own to buy

Mom!

This is the money I saved up to buy

Evening Scene

— Tan Baolian, Shanghai Zhirenyong Elementary School

The green trees on the embankment, the green mountains in the distance, and the tall pagoda reflect the red glow at the edge of the sky, making the evening scene even more lovely. At this time, in the garden, the tender green grass stands upright, waiting for the newly emerged moon; the shy morning glories hide in the foliage, much like shy children in the countryside, afraid to be seen. The few green bamboos planted outside the window laugh at the morning glories for not having the courage to raise their heads and greet the kind Moon Maiden.

The Leisurely and Comfortable Fat Pig

— Chu Jianping

A two-wheeled cart carried a fat pig with a fat head and big ears, leisurely moving along the road.

"How leisurely and comfortable! Since I came out of my mother's womb, I have always eaten and slept, never done anything. Now, I am even invited to sit in a cart and go out for a stroll. This is probably my natural blessing!" The fat pig said to itself very complacently.

Before long, its cart was pushed into a narrow hut. At this time, its sense of smell suddenly detected a very pungent fishy smell, but it was used to being comfortable, so it had no intention of studying the source of this fishy smell.

"That's not bad! I've always disliked the damp ground and have long wanted to get a bed to sleep on!" It thought to itself optimistically when someone put it on a bench. But in an instant, its throat suddenly felt icy cold, and at the same time, hot blood splattered, piercing its lungs. Only then did it understand; but what was the use of understanding?

Dear children! After reading this story, do you still want to be leisurely and comfortable and afraid of work?

Small Experiences

Empty Ink Bottle

Our ink is used up, but isn't there still an [empty ink bottle]? Let's not throw away this [empty bottle]; let's collect them. When we have collected about five or six, we can buy some paint ourselves (about ten copper coins), mix it evenly with boiling water, and make ink. Then carefully pour the mixed ink into each bottle, and it will become five or six full bottles of ink again. After the ink is used up again, don't throw away the [empty bottle]; collect another five or six, and do it again according to the previous method. By doing this continuously, the [empty ink bottles] we use can save us a lot of money.

Ink Remnants

— Jianfen

The black ink we use is very long when we first buy it, but after using it every day, it becomes shorter day by day, until there is no place to hold it, and it becomes a piece of [ink remnant]. Of course, this piece of [ink remnant] cannot be used for grinding. Should we throw it away? It feels like a pity. Now there is a method that can make it not wasted at all; that is, put the [ink remnant] in a bottle and add an appropriate amount of water; the [ink remnant] will slowly dissolve and turn into very good [ink].

The Beaks of Birds

— Yu Bailu

Birds are not like humans; they have no hands, only two feet. Children! Can you guess what they use to replace them? Feet can only be used for standing, wings can only be used for flying, only the beak is left. Yes, they use their beaks as hands. How do they use them? Let me tell you a few ways, and you can observe and guess the rest yourself.

Duck: You often see ducks. They have a wide beak, and the inside of the beak is soft. Therefore, even in murky muddy water, it can use the soft interior to distinguish the things it contains, just like our fingers. Also, because there are small tooth-like holes on the edge of its beak, when searching for food at the bottom of the water, it just randomly takes a mouthful of mud. When it sticks its head out of the water, it moves its beak slightly, so the muddy water flows out, and the remaining small fish and snails stay inside and are used as food.

Tailorbird: I know you all know that birds use their beaks to build nests, but you may not know how a tailorbird builds its nest. It uses the leaves of a large tree to fold into a tube shape, makes holes with its beak, and then finds fallen cotton, sews it up like thread. It can also raise three or four small birds inside, but this kind of bird is not very big.

Woodpecker: It relies on its sharp and hard beak to drill holes in tree trunks to find small insects that corrode the tree. If you hear the "tat-tat" sound of it pecking wood, don't drive it away, because it is beneficial to the tree.

Walking Stick Bird: It can be said to use its beak in the most peculiar way. Its beak is very long. In addition to using it for eating food, it often stands the tip of its beak upright on the ground when it is tired, just like an old man supporting himself with a wooden cane.

············

Children, you probably understand the beaks of birds!

Earthquake

— Xishi

Children, do you know that in past years, we donated money to help our enemies—the Japanese earthquake? Now let me talk about earthquakes.

The earth we live on was initially like fire. Later, it gradually solidified from the outside, becoming a layer of cold shell. Inside, however, it is still like molten material. The earth's crust has different thicknesses, so it often undergoes contraction and expansion. If the contraction or expansion of one part is faster than the contraction or expansion of another part, then cracks or explosions occur. The earth is affected and vibrates, which is an earthquake. Countless years ago, the ground rose up to form mountains. The ground at the bottom of the mountains is very thin, and the molten rock often erupts from the thinnest point. This is called a volcano. There are many in Japan. When it erupts, it can also cause earthquakes.

Miss Willow's Letter to Miss Spring Breeze — Ziming

Miss Spring Breeze:

Before talking to you, let me [stand at attention] here and give you a [90-degree] bow to express my gratitude for the grace of [rebirth]! I hope you will accept it!

I was being oppressed by Winter and could barely breathe, feeling dizzy as if I were dead, losing all sense. One day, I vaguely remembered that a gentle girl kissed me and comforted me. I felt a warm sensation on my body. This girl also combed my hair and put on green clothes for me. From then on, I actually woke up and met the world again. But I didn't know what kind of person that girl was. Later, Little Oriole told me that the kind person who knew me was you, Miss Spring Breeze!

Little Oriole comes to me every day. She is also a kind and lovely person who is very good at talking. Her voice is very beautiful, so many people like her. However, according to what she said to me, "[If Miss Spring Breeze doesn't come out to dominate the world, I would rather be mute for life!]" Ah! Miss Spring Breeze, I know now that you are not only my benefactor, but the midwife of all things! No wonder many stiff and dormant neighbors are now nodding and bowing to hold welcome parties!

The world of killing has changed, changed into a green world of flowers, a beautiful world!

Miss Spring Breeze, you are a meritorious person for living things, the ruler of the universe. I hope you will forever spread your grace to the world! Goodbye, Miss! Your Willow, who will never forget you all day long:

Miss Spring Breeze's Reply

— Ziming

Miss Willow:

Receiving your letter gives me the deepest comfort in my heart. Before reading the full text, I will of course stand at attention and raise my hand to give you a Boy Scout salute. However, I hope you won't do this again in the future. We will have many opportunities to meet!

What [grace of rebirth]? That's too flattering! I saw the living things in the world, and they were really pitiful! They were beaten by Granny Winter until their skin was broken and bleeding. The weak ones couldn't withstand her power and lay down on the ground for a long time, but that was also straightforward. However, those friends who were half-alive, half-dead, trembling, made my heart ache and caused me to shed tears of sympathy.

This aroused my motivation to come and dominate this world.

At first, I used an extremely sincere attitude to discuss with Granny Winter and told her about the situation of my friends being frozen, but she not only ignored me but became angry out of shame and intensified her oppression of living things. Therefore, I had no choice but to put on a stern face and directly fight against her.

Miss Willow, ah! Her iron fist was really fierce, and I almost failed. Fortunately, I had a full of enthusiasm and a continuous spirit, so she had no choice but to slip away.

Since she has slipped away, naturally, I have a duty to come and dominate this world: in addition to you, I also want to awaken all the people! The man-made world is too hypocritical. I want to use natural power to decorate it into a beautiful world. Miss Willow, follow the beat of Little Oriole's song and dance wildly! Goodbye.

May Little Oriole be equally happy, your Spring Breeze:

A New Clothes

— Ge Youfeng, Third Grade Student, Yangxi Shangzhi Elementary School, Xuxi

One day, my mother was preparing to make a new clothes for me and asked me what kind of cloth I liked. I suggested to her: "[Broadcloth and gabardine are foreign goods, I don't like them. I want domestic cloth. ]" My mother listened and agreed very much.

The next day, she asked my brother to go to the city to buy me snow-shame cloth. Snow-shame cloth has good color, a fair price, and is domestic goods.

The new clothes were made, and I wore them to school. Mr. Hu saw them and was extremely happy. He commended me at the morning meeting. And he told the students that if they make new clothes in the future, they should also learn from me and buy domestic cloth. From then on, the new clothes worn by the students were also made of domestic cloth one by one. Children all over the country! We must all be of one mind. Whether now or in the future, it is best to use domestic cloth when making new clothes!

Japanese Tennis Player Sato's Suicide Leads to Accusations Against the Tennis Association, Valuing Appearances Over Sato's Difficulties, Search for Body Lasts Seven Hours Without Success

(Japan United Press, 7th dispatch from Tokyo) Sato Jiro's older brother, Taro, received the tragic news of Sato's suicide and took a train to Tokyo that night to meet with members of the Tennis Association to discuss the aftermath. Mr. Taro told reporters, "I did not object to Jiro's trip to Europe this time, but Jiro himself actually did not want to go. However, due to the great responsibility, he decided to embark on the journey. Thinking of my younger brother, I could not help but feel pity. Now that things have come to this, I do not want to complain, but the content of the association's telegram ordering him to continue to Europe from Singapore put too much responsibility on my younger brother. The telegram stated that the association is currently raising funds from all parties, so returning midway would create difficulties for the association, etc. I have entrusted the association to telegraph Captain Genmaru to send all of Jiro's belongings from Singapore."

All Parties Criticize the Tennis Association

(Japan United Press, Tokyo, 7th dispatch) The Japanese Tennis Association's selection of Sato, who suffered from neurasthenia, as a player for this year's Davis Cup has led to his suicide. Now, criticism of the Tennis Association is growing. Sato left Japan with his illness after being selected as a player and embarked on the expedition. However, his condition worsened midway, and he disembarked in Singapore and telegraphed the association requesting permission to return home. However, the association authorities valued appearances and disregarded Sato's difficulties, ordering him to go to Europe. This shows a lack of compassion, it is said.

(Japan United Press, Tokyo, 7th dispatch) Sato's suicide note consists of five letters. Among them, the letters to Nishimura and Yamagishi briefly stated, "I hope you will work together with Miki-kun to strive for victory. I believe you will surely achieve your goals."

Circumstances Before and After Sato's Suicide

(Japan United Press, 7th dispatch from Tokyo) After receiving the news of Sato's suicide, the Japan United Press, due to the significant impact of this issue on the Japanese sports world, specially requested Captain Hakone Maru to report the circumstances before and after Sato's suicide. The reply was received on the 7th. The telegram is as follows: "Hakone Maru, sent at 11 PM on the 6th. Before the ship arrived in Singapore on the morning of the 4th, Sato suddenly requested permission from the purser to disembark and return home. The other three players, upon hearing this, tried their best to persuade Sato to abandon the idea of returning home. However, Sato explained his reasons, stating that he had been lacking concentration recently, and in this state, he would definitely not be able to participate in the competition, and that he was currently physically and mentally fatigued and did not want to continue the voyage, and planned to return home to rest and recuperate. Therefore, everyone recognized that the matter was unavoidable, and allowed him to disembark. Sato immediately disembarked in Singapore with all his luggage. However, that evening, Sato came to the original ship again and told people that he had changed his plans and would continue the voyage. Everyone suspected that Sato had received advice from other sources. On the 5th, before dawn, the ship left Singapore and headed for Singapore. Sato took a walk on the deck that day and was in good spirits. He practiced tennis in the afternoon and went to his room to sleep after dinner. At 8:30 PM, a ship's servant saw Sato take off his pajamas and put on Western clothes. However, at 11:30 PM, when Yamagishi, his roommate, entered the room, he did not see Sato. He searched all parts of the ship with the other two players, but could not find him. He then informed the purser. After a search by all the crew members, a suicide note was found. It was then presumed that he had committed suicide. The captain immediately ordered the ship to turn back and search the ocean surface for seven hours, but the body was not found. He had no choice but to continue sailing towards Singapore."

Athletes From Various Countries Shocked and Appalled

(Japan United Press, 7th dispatch from Tokyo) According to telegrams from England, America, and France to various countries, the tennis circles of various countries were shocked and appalled upon receiving the news of Sato's suicide. They all regretted the loss of Japan's most outstanding tennis player.

(Havas Agency, Berlin, 6th dispatch) Japanese tennis player Sato Jiro, who came to Europe from Japan to participate in the Davis Cup competition, unexpectedly jumped into the sea after the ship left Singapore due to neurasthenia. According to reports, when Japan and Germany held the Davis Cup competition last year, Sato and Buri represented Japan and defeated Germany, and his skills were excellent, earning the sympathy of the German people. The sports circles here were deeply saddened by the news.

(Havas Agency, New York, 6th dispatch) After the news of the tragic death of Japanese Davis Cup player Sato reached here, the president of the American Tennis Association, Morihael, expressed his condolences, saying that Sato was his friend and a frank and upright player. Sato's death has weakened the tennis world, he said. Major tennis players in San Francisco were also deeply shocked. Madam Madi and others all praised Sato's skills, saying that his tragic death was a misfortune for the tennis world.

Number of People Receiving Primary Education Per 10,000 People, Canada is the Most, China is the Least

The Ministry of Education has compiled statistics on the status of primary education in various provinces and cities in the 19th year (of the Republic), and has also compiled a comparison of the status of primary education in various countries from 1927 to 1931 as follows: The number of people receiving primary education per 10,000 people is calculated. China has 236 people, which is the least. Canada has 2,082 people, which is the most. Next is Australia with 1,801 people, the United States with 1,768 people, the Netherlands with 1,649 people, Japan with 1,582 people, the United Kingdom with 1,580 people, Switzerland with 1,439 people, Norway with 1,392 people, Belgium with 1,322 people, Denmark with 1,244 people, Poland with 1,233 people, Italy with 1,230 people, Sweden with 1,135 people, Germany with 1,125 people, France with 1,088 people, Austria with 1,071 people, Spain with 1,060 people, and Soviet Russia with 834 people.

The 8th International Philosophical Conference is scheduled to be held in Prague, Czechoslovakia, in September of this year. Overview of Primary Schools and Kindergartens in Various Provinces and Cities Since the Founding of the Republic of China

The Ministry of Education has investigated the overview of primary schools (including senior and junior) and kindergartens in various provinces and cities from the founding of the Republic of China to the 19th year (of the Republic), and has compiled the following statistical comparisons.

(1) Number of primary schools and kindergartens: The total number of schools in various provinces and cities across the country was 86,318 in the first year (of the Republic), 107,286 in the second year, 121,081 in the third year, 128,525 in the fourth year, 120,097 in the fifth year, 177,751 in the 11th year, 212,385 in the 18th year, and 250,840 in the 19th year. The number of schools in the 19th year increased by 154,522 compared to the first year, and increased by 38,455 compared to the 18th year. (2) Number of children in primary schools and kindergartens: 2,795,475 in the first year, 3,485,807 in the second year, 3,921,727 in the third year, 4,140,066 in the fourth year, 3,843,454 in the fifth year, 6,601,802 in the 11th year, 8,882,077 in the 18th year, and 10,948,979 in the 19th year. The number of children in the 19th year increased by 8,153,504 compared to the first year, and increased by 2,066,902 compared to the 18th year. (3) Annual expenditure on primary schools and kindergartens: 19,334,480 yuan in the first year, 23,531,124 yuan in the second year, 24,899,807 yuan in the third year, 23,881,730 yuan in the fourth year, 23,497,097 yuan in the fifth year, 31,449,963 yuan in the 11th year, 64,721,025 yuan in the 18th year, and 89,416,977.28 yuan in the 19th year. The expenditure in the 19th year increased by 70,082,497.28 yuan compared to the first year, and increased by 24,695,952.28 yuan compared to the 18th year.

(Note) The number of schools increased by more than 38,000 this year, the number of children increased by more than 2,060,000, and the expenditure increased by more than 24,000,000. The number of children receiving compulsory education increased by 4.97 percentage points (the total number of school-age children in the country is 49,116,060, and the number of children who have received and are currently receiving compulsory education is 10,844,131, accounting for 22.07% this year). In addition to a few provinces and cities slightly decreasing, most of the above items have increased compared to previous years. The most increase was in Guangdong, with an increase of 8,117 schools and 6,055,668 yuan, and in Shandong, with an increase of 603,338 children.

City Schools Promote the New Life Movement

Inspection by Representatives from the Promotion Association and the Education Bureau

The Shanghai Municipal New Life Movement Promotion Association resolved to hold a New Life Movement promotion week starting April 9th. The first day (the 9th) is designated as School Promotion Day. The Promotion Association has sent a letter to the Municipal Education Bureau requesting all schools to comply and implement the initiative. Representatives will be dispatched to various schools for inspection. The promotion methods are as follows: (1) Each school should report on the meaning of the New Life Movement during the weekly memorial service for the late Premier, and also read out the New Life Public Pledge; (2) conduct a thorough cleaning within the school; (3) inspect students' bodies, clothing, desks, chairs, and school supplies to ensure cleanliness; (4) select students to form a propaganda team to promote the New Life Movement in the vicinity; (5) create a New Life environment within the school; (6) elementary schools should create a unit on "[Implementing New Life in Teaching]"; (7) the principal or student union officers should solicit members for the Promotion Association on behalf of the association, and prepare to establish branches; (8) urge day students to promote the New Life Public Pledge to their families; (9) representatives from the general association and the Education Bureau will be dispatched to inspect the progress of each school.

Women's Garden, Issue 8

The Second Stage

— Xu Xizhen

In these turbulent years, some progressive women who care about their own problems, even with extraordinary efforts, cannot avoid a kind of sorrow of being lost in the fog.

This phenomenon does not mean that women in general have lost their way on the road to liberation; but rather that they voluntarily remain in this stage.

When rebellious women began to feel the oppression of intolerable ethics and customs, they bravely raised this question themselves. From reality, they realized that all the old ethics and unreasonable social systems were built on an economic foundation. Thus, they further began to strive for economic independence and raised the banner of [Women's Economic Independence].

Because they wanted to practice this slogan, ordinary women all wanted to find a job: whether as clerks or laborers, as long as there was a job, as long as they could be economically independent, it seemed that all women's problems could be solved at this point. Not to mention distant things, even thirty years ago, ordinary intellectual women and scholars studying women's issues all firmly believed that [as long as there is a job, women have their own economic ability, and at the same time can get all the liberation]. And in China, didn't all the intellectual women around the May Fourth Movement accept this principle without any doubt?

As a result, many [professional women] emerged in society.

However, through experience, they learned a new lesson: professional women still feel a sense of shameful failure.

Sincere women pursuing independence, they are not difficult to realize the special role of shops employing female employees; in China, we can see the facts that professional women are subjected to special insults and manipulation, tens of thousands of women are struggling under the insulting term [vase] with a painful heart for the sake of life, and on the other hand, we can also hear the facts that some female employees have been suspended for refusing the manager's special requirements.

This is not a special situation in Chinese society, and the same phenomenon is also revealed in American society, which has the title of [professional women] as the supreme honor; female employees receive the manager's dinner invitation, no matter what important things they have, they always have to go. In addition, such as dancers, waitresses in restaurants, movie actresses, etc., although they have a job, they are still living in the male society, this is a fact.

As a result, they all realized that: having a job is still suppressed by men, and true independence is still not available. They struggled out of the cage of the family, from the palms of their husbands, and went to society to work, but the result was still in the hands of men, but flew from one cage to another.

The modern women's movement has long been stuck in this gray stage.

In a patriarchal society, the husband is the object of direct oppression and struggle against women, so they all think that having a job and leaving the husband will solve all problems. In fact, everything will not be so simple. Undoubtedly, from the lessons of reality, modern women should all understand that the so-called [women's liberation] is definitely not just a victory over the husband in the family. After they have completed the first stage, they must work harder to continue their more difficult second stage, and further struggle against the unreasonable system of the old society, otherwise it is definitely impossible for women to achieve reasonable liberation.

Moreover, in this era when everything is impossible, almost all problems have become common problems for people. Therefore, women's liberation is not a ridiculous comedy of [male and female struggle]. Mrs. Beard, a scholar of women's issues in the United States, said in an article [The End of Women's Rights]: [Women have left the broad exploration of life and are working hard to win against men in a narrow way. Taking the rights and freedoms of men as the object, working hard to move forward, trying to get the same rights and freedoms as men, this is almost the only way for all women's rights movements. Because of this, they ignored the dangers of the future and were confused by the current opponent. This is like two people flying kites, the man's kite is in front, and the woman's kite is desperately chasing from behind, she ignores everything, she just wants to catch up with the kite in front, or even surpass it. As for all the changes in the wind and clouds in front of the man's kite, they will not think of or see them.] She also said: [For example, women demand equal pay for men and women in factories, but what is the use when men and women cannot find jobs in factories?] From this, we can see that: when everything becomes a problem, women's liberation should (and only) start with obtaining a reasonable social system in a broad sense, in order to achieve the expected success. Although this is a long-term promissory note, it is fully redeemable.

Of course, it is not to deny the necessity of women's liberation in the family; it is mostly ridiculous for women to engage in social movements in the hands of their husbands and in the accumulation of housework, but the purpose of this article is only to point out that after women are liberated from the family, it is only the first stage on the road to the entire liberation, and in order to get the overall liberation, they still cannot ignore the second stage and turn their attention to the social system.

Opinions of World Thinkers on Women's Issues (1)

— Hua

I. Condorcet

When the modern women's movement was still in its infancy, the first to pay attention to it was Condorcet, the last of the great French philosophers of the eighteenth century. Born in 1743 and died in 1794, he was a great thinker and politician of France at that time, proficient in mathematics and astronomy, and was a participant in the historically famous French Encyclopedia. At the age of thirty, he actively participated in various social movements: when the French Revolution began (1789), he was one of the very active leaders. After the revolution, he was elected as a member of the [Legislative Assembly].

In 1787, Condorcet published a famous book called A Citizen of New Haven's Letter, which contained an essence of text on the equality of men and women, which roughly said: Women are also like men, endowed with emotions, and have the heart to distinguish between good and evil, so women should enjoy equal rights with men, etc. He advocated that women should have the right to vote and be elected, and expressed a hope that women should hold all social positions, which should not be prohibited by law. As a result, the theory of equality between men and women began to attract attention.

In 1788, Condorcet published another article in JournaledelaSociele, advocating that women should enjoy all the rights of citizens.

As mentioned earlier, Condorcet was a celebrity in French society at that time, so after he advocated the theory of equality between men and women, French women, who were still oppressed by the feudal system, were awakened and enthusiastically praised Condorcet's proposition and worked hard to promote its realization. At that time, under the wave of the revolution, women's groups appeared in Paris and major cities in various provinces one after another. These groups, they hoped to become a force that influences national legislation, public autonomous organs, and the entire social life, and [fulfill the command of heaven,] and help establish a civic rational state. They advocated that women should fulfill equal obligations and enjoy equal rights. The enthusiastic activists of these women's groups were Gu Marie, the details of which will be described in a special article later, which will not be mentioned here.

The theory of equality between men and women seems to be very bland and unremarkable now. More than 140 years ago, not to mention in our ancient China, even in France before the revolution, this theory was regarded as a flood beast, because at that time France was still under the rule of the feudal system, the idea of [men are superior to women] shrouded people's concepts, women were completely in a position of being oppressed in social customs, and had no rights at all in economy, law, and politics. Since Condorcet advocated the theory of equality between men and women, women's social status began to reveal a glimmer of dawn. So the modern women's movement originated in the era of the French Revolution, but the initiator of the idea of women's liberation should be Condorcet!

However, Condorcet's first advocacy of the theory of equality between men and women in history was not because he relied on his intelligence and fabricated it out of thin air, but had its social and economic background. This background is the alternation of new and old societies in France at that time, the paragraph of the old feudal system and the rise of new production methods - capitalism. He, Condorcet, happened to be in this era, experiencing that the emerging social and economic system needed women's liberation, needed women to be educated, and came to society, so he was prescient, conformed to the requirements of the times, and advocated that women should have equal rights with men. When we study the thoughts of each famous figure in history, we should first pay attention to his social background, which is very important.

Is Marriage a Woman's Career?

— Girlfriend

I seem to remember that a certain Mr. published the grand theory that marriage is a woman's only career in a certain publication not long ago. But the day before yesterday, when I read Ms. Wanxiang's article [Talking about the Relationship between Women and Career] in the special issue of Women and Career in the Female Youth Monthly, I couldn't help but be confused.

Ms. Wanxiang said affirmatively in her paper: Marriage is definitely not a woman's career. Is marriage a woman's career after all? Or the only career? For this question, I think it is really necessary to re-determine and study it!

Of course, saying that marriage is a woman's only career also has their so-called many reasons. However, there is only one truth. Which side is correct? In order to make the problem more clear, I think it is necessary to explain in advance what exactly is a career? The meaning of this term.

What is a career? [Directly speaking: the so-called explanation of making a living can be regarded as a career, ordinary people often say to find a job when seeking a career to find a job] This is Mr. [Winter]'s high opinion on the issue of career in his masterpiece [The Great Mission of Women's Marriage] on the supplement of this newspaper. But is this explanation correct? Obviously, this is not correct? Because for whatever question, we should never only make superficial observations, or only follow the stale views of the general world. We must stand on the position of social science, understand and analyze from an economic point of view, and then we can insight into the true meaning of the problem.

Of course, in the current society, most people usually interpret career as a [rice bowl] for maintaining life, but science tells us that common sense is not necessarily correct? The correct solution of all problems still depends on science.

Therefore, for the question of what exactly is a career, we strictly analyze it from the point of view of economics, it is just a part of the social production labor division.

The wild chickens on Sima Road sell their bodies to maintain their lives, although most people think that this is also a career, but in the economic sense, it cannot be regarded as a career at all? Because that is just a kind of deformed thing unique to the corrosive part of the current unreasonable private system.

Since the definition of career is as described above, then it is very obvious whether marriage is a woman's career.

Of course, we also understand very well that saying [marriage] is a woman's only career has an insulting and satirical meaning, because in the current social environment, most women, even those who were able to be economically independent before marriage, mostly give up supporting themselves after marriage and completely rely on men, since most people think that being able to maintain life is a career, it is no wonder that a certain Mr. wants to shout: Marriage is a woman's only career.

According to the above explanation, our final conclusion is: Ms. Wanxiang recognizes that [marriage is definitely not a woman's career, marriage is just the starting point of the common life of men and women]. It is absolutely correct, as for saying that marriage is a woman's only career, this kind of argument, in our opinion, is not only a wrong worldly prejudice, but also a malicious satire for ordinary women!

Before and After

— Liang

| Fragments of Life |

I remember it was seven or eight years ago, when I was still in school; at that time my life was well-off, and my heart was naive and pure. Based on my sentimental nature, and more influenced by the cultivation of literature, I yearned for an ideal life - the dream of love supremacy. The world's fame and profit, in my opinion, are all external things, insignificant. People's desires often need a satisfaction that transcends the material - the spiritual, I often think this way. At that time, my only hope was to have a lover with noble thoughts and personality, not confined by things, not moved by circumstances, and full of enthusiasm. Poverty is not a concern, and poverty is not a worry. As long as there is a sacred love that transcends everything, I can abandon everything and sacrifice everything, and be intoxicated in the beautiful, gentle, and poetic realm of love for the rest of my life.

Starting from this point of view, I searched for my life partner, and soon found him among my classmates. His paper was a powerful medium for me to know him. It was a piece of scenery writing and emotional expression, the beautiful words and transcendent thoughts deeply attracted me. My emotional soul could not tolerate the restraint of reason, so from then on, I recognized him as the character in my ideal, and at the same time, I knew his attitude of being studious and thoughtful, and his unconventional views, which increased my respect and love for him; after a considerable period of acquaintance, we officially became engaged and practiced cohabitation love. After cohabitation, the time of contact increased, and gradually both sides discovered many differences in temperament, habits, and thoughts. As time went by, such discoveries became more and more, and many times even caused conflicts because of this. Of course, our love suffered a great twist, and my soul also suffered a great blow. What made me the most painful was that all my ideals were shattered. When a person once overturns his beliefs and breaks everything, what is left is only vastness and emptiness, so he wanders and hesitates on the fork in the road of life. My situation at that time was like this, disappointed and sad, obviously I had fallen into the abyss of pain.

After many struggles, I finally raised my head from this dark abyss and saw a brighter way out. That is, I understood the mistakes of the past and the path to be taken in the future. In today's society where material is the center of gravity, all human activities are dominated and influenced by its power, and love is of course no exception. This kind of idealistic love is just a story described in literature, and cannot be seen in reality. My disappointment is nothing more than the ideal is too high and not suitable for the actual reason. To avoid pain, we should start from reality, and not waste energy for the sake of ethereal ideals.

Speaking of life, in addition to love - it is just a corner of life, and cannot generalize its entirety - there is a broader meaning and a more important mission. Since people are social animals and a member of society, they should all serve the majority of people in society based on their innate abilities. To be disappointed and passive for the sake of love is not only a loss to the individual, but also a loss to society.

Now, the heavy shadows pressing on my heart - disappointment, sadness, and passivity - have been removed one by one. New courage and new spirit are pushing me forward on the path of life.

Japanese Women Oppose New Taxes

Tokyo Correspondence

| Activities of the Municipal Purification League |

Amidst the general [depression], [deficit budgets] are found everywhere. Tokyo, the largest city in Japan, cannot escape this fate either. The debt at the end of the ninth year of Showa (this year) increased to a staggering amount, reaching the gate of 900 million yen, which made it impossible to turn its head. In order to cover up this mess, the municipal authorities decided to add six new taxes, which are expected to increase revenue by 3.5 million yen. The Women's Municipal Purification League, in which Ms. Shizuichi Kato and others participated, opposed the [special income tax] and [employment tax] in these six new taxes from the standpoint of women. Their reasons are: the special income tax is intended to seize the wallets of low-income people whose income is 600 yen and are now exempt from paying national tax, although it is the product of the cry of the deficit Tokyo City, it is not allowed. As for the employment tax, although it is nominally called the employment tax, among the 118,588 taxpayers, only 5,884 are men (accountants and errand boys), which is essentially equivalent to a maid tax. Whether for families employing maids or for the maids themselves, this new tax is not allowed. For example, in a situation where both husband and wife have to find jobs to make a living due to living conditions, then nanny has become a necessity in life, not a luxury. If a housewife has to dismiss the maid due to the taxation of this new tax, she will return to the family from society, which is not to say that it is a loss for women in society. From the maids themselves, they will be more threatened by unemployment by this new tax, and even if they are not unemployed, they will suffer from the pain of intensified labor and reduced wages.

In this way, they insisted on opposing the increase of these two new taxes, and elected representatives to visit the municipal authorities to demand the abolition of the original proposal. The municipal authorities, however, have different opinions, believing that families employing people are mostly property-owning classes and have the ability to bear a considerable amount of tax. Therefore, the tax regulations stipulate that all those under the age of 16 and over the age of 60, or those suffering from disability and temporary nurses, are generally required to pay the following tax rates. That is, employing one person, paying 5 yen per year, 7 yen for two people, 10 yen for three people, 13 yen for four people, 16 yen for five people, 20 yen for six people, 24 yen for seven people, 28 yen for eight people, 33 yen for nine people, and 40 yen for ten people (calculated per servant), if more than ten people are used, 2 yen should be added for each additional person. It is estimated that 746,923 yen can be raised annually.

For Tokyo City, which is struggling under extreme poverty, this is indeed a good piece of fat. Therefore, it has quite the intention to kick away the women's resistance and implement the new tax.

Future Female Aviators

— Zhang Zhiru

Ms. Qiaoyun, the daughter of Mr. Wang Zhaosong, a Justice of the Peace in Kuala Lumpur, British Malaya, has recently joined the Kuala Lumpur Flying Club as a flying member. The news has not only shocked the Chinese women's community but has also been greatly praised by people from all walks of life in Malaya.

Ms. Wang is a Straits Chinese born in Kuala Lumpur. She is currently twenty years old. Her biological mother has passed away. At the age of six, she followed her father back to her ancestral home in Guangzhou, and after visiting Hong Kong, returned to Southeast Asia. At the age of fourteen, she graduated from the Kan Cheng Elementary School in Kuala Lumpur and then entered the Methodist Girls' School. She is currently studying in the eighth grade, diligently pursuing her studies, and is respected and loved by her teachers and classmates.

Seeing that few Chinese women dared to take risks, Ms. Wang requested her parents to let her study aviation. Initially, her family strongly opposed it. After many twists and turns and a long period of time, she persistently requested it in a tactful, decisive, and sincere manner, and finally achieved her goal. Now, after school every day, she drives her private car to the airfield to practice piloting with pilot Mr. Newall. She said that once her skills are proficient, she will gather like-minded people to organize a commercial airmail service to connect the air routes of Central and Southern China.

Women's Topics

— Dubu

An Example of British Female Workers

Regardless of East or West, ancient or modern, women are known to be talkative. But what exactly do they talk about? The statistics were compiled from a recent survey by the British Industrial Health Bureau, with the surveyed subjects being British working women, especially those in the labor force. The central question of the study was what they talk about in the workplace. The survey period was fifty-four weeks, which took a year, and was obtained through scientific and precise questionnaires.
